    Folio 1v Dhandhanggula //0//oṃ awig̈nanam astu ya nama siḍĕm //0//

    1.

    apasaṅ tabe kamy amariñci hamijilakĕn tatyani smara ḍpuri sabda kaṅ pinet muḍa tan wri ri la/ku rag̈a mily aƞi/kĕt karasmin ṣapun tan iƞapura dera saṅ tame wruḥ, kumawi haṙsamet raras kumaliƞa 1+lad. w1+j1+l1+ sand1+ t1+las1+ra
    /wirasaṅƞnira saṅƞ adi ḍaṅḍaṅgula tĕmbaṅni wacana tan riṅƞ pupuḥ tirwan amet mahaṙdikani tĕmbuṅ, panalamuṙ medrani budi rag̈agĕṅ kalƞĕṅƞan. wuṙyyan manaḥ jinu/m. syaḥ śiṙṇa cipta ƞambara pingatanityasa rusit paṅnalemor i driya
    ø jumawanut swarani sukṣmalit pan alamuṙ cipta daṙpa muk.skaṙ ḋibya/ huyaṅ kemuṙ make swĕḥ dyatan malulut kiraṅ yoga pramada lwiḥ, winoteṅ kanuragan. jñaṇa salaḥ surup. ḍaṙsaṇa tṛṣṇa nityasaḥ tan kagiwaṅ sumĕk pa/macanaṇi siḥ dyaniƞ amriḥ carita
    ø nahan ṣaṅsiptaniƞ amarici saṅƞ amaƞgiḥ tusṭa moṅ kawiṙyan riṅ wilatikta pranaḥe pralabda prabu wĕruḥ watĕ/k dana mule kasiḥ sasi hasikĕp kasusilan pramaṙtya budy alus puspita nĕmpu kakala kasub kaṛƞĕ hapuṇya hadana lwiḥ boga sadana lumraḥ
    ø /tlas denira mukti/ kasmin winusan denira saṅƞ atiṅkaḥ makana tuwa wayaḥe tuẗug.waṙtini tuwuḥ luwaṙ tanṣaḥ muṙti sumilib śamaya mageḥ prana mitani
    Folio 2rra larut     prama sukmani raga sidanika tan tigaṅ dina lawasniki hanahurakĕ pjaḥ
    ø hatigal tanaya hastri kakaliḥ lanaṅ tugal hapadudya maṙga putra gaṇa/ wikan i reḥ saṅ ti/bra lampus hamupusi pura sumiwi sunu lanaṅ piniraṅ lagyanom tan wriṅ hyan tan ṣinuƞan raja yogya kasihanitya sinĕkuṅ mapan rare halit dalu tanpua/ puhara
    ø satatya larani daya rarya hanom hajeṅƞ uniƞa yena kramra sapa wogan iku tĕmbe yyaktiku hamulaƞuni kumara yayaḥe pasti taha/kna maṅke sadeni ƞadu matikaḥ kraptini jñana haguṅṛnan hana make ki siƞamada hali tan. wruḥ sanake nora sudi mapan taƞgal. yayaḥ maṙmani/tan mule
    ø wuwusĕn ki siƞamada kari katigal pjaḥ wyaṙni bapa nastapa, hapuhara ƞel. ya sebya lampus kawlas aṙṣa duka priyatin ramestri/ tumut abela kari tanpa nusu saṅṣara maṅsi lara kaṅnastapa hanaƞis rahina wƞi yayaḥ bu makasambat.
    ø saṅ kakaṅ histri kaliḥ hamukti kapal. smu mĕ/denira śaṅ suka mankin tan. ketaṅ harine ki siƞamada lusuḥ siṅ woṅ sudi hamilasani saya tuwa riṅ wayaḥ sasipta wri laku, nisṭani rag̈a karasa/ winiweka duka nasta/pane lwiḥ syarasani waṙdaya
    ø ƞ kadaṅ wṛgane tan ana sudi siƞamada sinĕgya panas maṙmmaniƞ anistan. wri deṣa, parani laku l1+ƞa
    Folio 2v iimpus tan pamit.     luƞha sakiṅ pradesa lpas lampaḥhipun. ri wanapriga kahaṙsa duṙgama ḃaya kewĕḥ wyaṙ tan kahisṭi dahat gĕṅniṅ kalaran.
    ø /saya lpas tan ana/ katoliḥ cipta laƞ1+t lampus niṅ katṛsṇa hanṣĕl. rag̈a dan liƞe katuwun. wakisun ṣaṣayani rag̈a tan ṣipi tan. wruḥ riṅ
    Folio 2v rama rena,     nastapa huwu huwuḥ haƞiṅ kawaśaha huga raganiṅsun. mon kagugu kagoraweṅ riṅ wƞi tuwas siƞit/. rag̈a tan wruḥ ƞenaka
    ø kunaṅ yen ana kĕsĕliṅƞ ati baya luhuṅ haƞuśiya wana make, nusupa riṅ ƞo make pjaḥha luhuṙriṅ/ gunuṅ yan mijila wacanana niki nawiniwedaka riṅ nala rumupe riṅƞ ayu, datan kawaṙnaha riṅ maṙga talaś laris lampanwa/ hasaƞu taƞis prasta jĕṅ riṅ prawata
    ø hamaƞgiḥ ḍukuḥ welahaṙja mikiṅƞakĕn maṙggā mulat ki siƞamada śaksana rere jĕṅ rapuḥ/ cipta maliḥ kapaƞgiḥ saṅ ta ligiḥ riṅ made, sambrama ki paƞuwusan hatanya risni wacana , bageya saṅ tami ḍataṅ mara/ ke, hañaṙ wikan. ƞoṅ kaki, lwir tanma priyatin polahe laḥ bapa maratiya, wriṅ naya ki siƞamada sami haliƞgiḥ, ki/ habĕt liṅnya taken, di sakan. teṅśun kaki sumahuṙr alon mawaraḥ pinakane
    ø tuhu tan. wikan wṛti/nta kami ƞoṅ bapā tanya śwapa namanta, waraḥ jati kami make, siƞamadya wriṅ smu saṅ tabe hanakta kaki, hapajar i nama
    Folio 3r     nawi tuhu tan wruḥ siƞamadḍya haraniṅ wwaṅ, dahat. deniṅ hamukti nastapa ḷwiḥ kawlas aṙśa nityasa
    ø haƞuśi ka/daṅ wṛga tan ana sudi tuhu dinaliḥ tikna wiruda, datan ana sudi kabeḥ, pjaḥ bapa rama hibu karakasa gwan i kari ki/ habĕt mawacana, haƞṛś. twasky aruƞu, śamono denta wacana, ki paƞuwusann aliṅ haƞṛs. raśaniƞ a/ti ki baru mareneya
    ø saṅ siksa prapta wot.skaṙ punapi kaṙyya ƞawe bwaha hadan pala bojanā depunaśereg/. saṅ tami hasmu ƞliḥ tan lagna ki baru mitaṙ lakw ag̈e, haglis lampahiƞ utusan. mdal punaṅ pupuḍutan sakul sa/tiḍan kalawan bitutu tetep laḥ ta bwakṣa saṅ tami tuww asamun bapa deniṅra pupude
    ø tan. wuwusĕn. denya bwuksa/ prapti heṙtali mugwiṅ talakā madaṅ samwa wusan tan asuwe hyaṅƞ aṙka mwaṅ kasurup na wulan saṅ tapa haliṅ, dipunsa/n.teṅśeṅ manaḥ sunya nikaṅ ḍukuḥ, siƞamadya mawacana hantyanta pan akaṙyya dibwa matitis. tuhw amṛtani jiwa
    ø ka
    Folio 3vpiṅluḥ śwaranira ki waśi     tan sipi maṙmanirā tumiƞal haƞṛs atine hatine mulat. waṙnnaniṅ tamu, ya ḍu/ḥ heman tan ana kṛtti nayā śolaḥ jatmika rupane habagus. punapa śakaniṅ luƞa, paśewaka priḥ rag̈anira/ nak mami malaṙ hamag̈wa lara
    ø siƞamaḋa hanampani wisṭi wikan parinayani wacana sumarapratyakṣe rate pasaṅ sarudi la
    Folio 3vku     ta katoliḥ rasmini gati kdĕḥniṅ cipta brata ƞoṅwaḥhana laku ƞowahana laku naƞi ketuṅ prasiḋahaniƞ akikin.ta weniṅ rag̈a nastapa
    ø me/lik tan. haṙsa kuraṅƞ a/mukti riƞ asewaka hakeḥ bayanya haṣwĕ lara guƞe sira saṅ janma lawu paratiṇḍa mewĕḥ haruci raka hyaṅ tan. wri naya hakol piṇḍa pu/guṅ tan kage solaḥ sowara tanpa saṇḍaṅ hakumul tuṙ kumalikiḥ haṅlud tanpa sadana
    ø waniḥ saṅƞ asewakaha hamriḥ kitri hamriḥ saṅ kawi suka sugiḥ/ya hakeḥ maṙgane hamosel. hapuhara hanugu, pulakṛti kaṅ denulati hapakṣa ƞadu titaḥ laḃa ḋenpalaku haƞi masa katkana/ haraƞkal. wisayane kagiri g̈iri kaƞelan amet ṣuka
    ø maṙmaniṅ rag̈a ƞusi wanadri haƞowana gĕṅni wisaya haja dene kadi maṅke lara/ lapa katĕmĕ sagonane sarira hiki nisṭa yen ṣampun titaḥ was ḋum awakisun ṣadeniƞ aṛp.lwiḥha raga nisṭa kapuraṅ deni pawṛti ha/ƞel. yen ulatana
    ø gantaṅ hupama raga, kḷĕm. kneṅ samudra maṅsa liwata hisine yen uwu takĕripun hamwĕhi lara kaseḥsiḥ mo/n. ton iƞ aniṅ/ sukāniƞ amukti rame tan apik pranaḥhiṅ laḃa, riṅ gunuṅ riṅƞ ampaḥ pasnĕtane hawrat kalabane haƞahub. soṙni pisis niṣṭa dama
    Folio 4rtan ana, pulakṛtinipun.
    ø pacĕ wṛadayanira hyaṅ wasi hamihaṙsa paśrani wacana hanom pratameṅƞ ujaṙre kasilib ciptanisun halaḥ/ dene rarya/ hanom. kawi lampus. tṛsna śarat hapakṣa ṛp laku, dibya malaṙ tape waṇa śrama kamhananira saṅ tapa sakti ḃikṣuka maƞan ṣukla
    ø pa/tya waṣa ƞoṅ kaki haƞalaṅƞi pratikaḥhira hasewaṇa ri sun apiṇḍa tan paweḥ mewĕḥ bapa ri laku lagwa wayaḥ kitanak mami riƞ aƞuśwakĕn./ brata hakweḥ bañcananipun panilibniṅ daśendriya, tapaśenaku ḃapa riṅƞ aƞawasi paƞuwusan i yoga
    ø sawaṅƞn ri pun i lampaḥ ka/ki sarira tan. kneṅ ƞaku juga wastunĕn makin asuwe tan pamana ewuh duṙgamaƞel maṙgan1+ k1+ tri nnolaḥ himaniman ṣira saṅ kṛtayu tan ka/slan anug̈raha tiwas bisa lakw ayu yu tan. kneṅƞ iṣṭi haron lumakṣanaha
    ø siƞamada hanakisun kaki wṛdi hati waspadeṅ paƞucap. wruḥ/ ri laku sabda mule haƞiṅ dipun.tumulus kawasakĕn raganta kaki priḥ śwara kaṅƞ utama ḍuḥ sawƞn ri pun. gĕṅniṅ tṛsna umoṙr i ra/ga tan. kna piṇu/raṅ saṅ hatapa sakti sampun. kṛtisamaya
    ø madrani latri kahaṙśa ki habĕt lagya wacaṇa mapitutuṙ prayogani lakw aƞne siƞa
    Folio 4vmaḋa nampani     kawƞan. ciptanira winaraḥ riṅ reḥ ayo kita kĕmbakĕmba lkasniṅ tapa mudita depunawas. glaṙri laku kaṅ pinet niṙ lkasniṅ wirati dana/punya yen tan. wruḥ/ panuṅgalane
    ø waniḥ bapa nata1+ƞ akikin hakweḥ ḃawa lkas. nora tapa milupra hiƞ apagawe śawaniḥ saƞ awiku hakeḥ silib ri la/ku kaki hawis putuseṅ wirasa pamatĕsiṅ wuwus adikara maƞan. kla tan lyen kaṅ denṣadya suka wiṙyya sugiḥ hamriḥ yoliḥhiṅ brata
    ø hana sarara/ga ƞel aƞli1+ madigini nityasa 1+ sukaniṅ pamṣukten. yeku tapa wulaƞun gĕṅniṅ tamaḥ ta kaṅ denulati haƞuripurip. driya/ ṣawisayaniṅ jabuṅ kasiliba menek wṛsaḥ ri laku lamon tan wruḥ parani sandi haƞaku gagajaran.
    ø tan makaṇa śwadyaniƞ akikin ṣaƞ amaṅƞgiḥ jati/ni wacana øiṙ ta suka lyan. pamukten hupaṛinbuṙ kalaƞni pawestri lwiḥ ka swaṙgani wiṙyyawan niṙ tan tṛsna lampus paƞimuṙniṅ tapa lana datan aƞe/l bapa lkasni ƞalampaḥhi priḥhĕn raṣa menaka
    ø siƞamaḋa ṛƞĕ tutuṙ mami riƞ anmu rasa haja wiha natarana sabda mule hatapa dentumulu/s manawaṙsa muliḥ/ hamukti saṅ wiku yen atatas tan ulahanisun manawa lipuṙ kaṅ manaḥta, budi lupa mawa kaṙyya cipta karasmin aṙsa waluya ƞampaḥ
    ø haneṅ ku
    Folio 5rna hanunuṅgal ṣakti     hatyata kawasa lumkas hakumandaṙma natare sita pabrata dentutuṙ dapa denya maƞun kasaktin kasṛk winoṙr i wig̈na hyaƞ anaṅga ƞimuṙ sida/ pinaliḥh ajñana salaḥ simpaṅ ciptane winor iƞ asi manasaṙ reƞ ala
    ø datan kawasa kṛtini budi hanuƞgal. jñana mareṅƞ ala, wwaṙ ta tutuṙ tanpa gawe sṙniṅ lulut ṣumaput. pamacanani rara śakti hawali ma/reƞ ampaḥ, keśaḥ kapalayu punika mewĕhi brata, iƞĕttiƞĕt ṣiƞamada hayo lali den.wruḥ riṅ lawa/n. rowaṅ
    ø lampaḥ hala hanak mami kapuraṅ deniṅ kṛtisamaya, śarira yen saƞarane tan wuruṅƞa katmu, hanacad. ṛ/gĕpĕn iṅƞ ati hapan. wĕtuniṅ duta makoliya tutuṙ tan koniƞa maniƞ ulaḥ saṅ praśida tuhu winady alampaḥhi budi ta/n kaslan
    ø waspadakĕn pekaṅ was.mṙti haja tiniru wiku goman iṅ daraḥ yyaṅkta ñoloṅ baśarane saṅ hyaṅƞ agama putu śa
    Folio 6rrira sama hakikin.     ñana dipunatuwa, ragĕkap kaṅ pamutus mapan wus praptame rasa, duluṙrana kṛti jatmikaja silib, pe/t sarasaniṅ taya
    ø siƞamada gaṙjiteṅƞ ati manampani wƞaniki śwara, wira cipta mirage makwa maƞgiḥ pamuwus. tutuṙ lwiḥ mawara/ḥ yukti śabda paruwat mala, siƞamada muwus paƞeran tulusakna dera waraḥ kacaṙyya rasaniṅƞ ati manira nuta lampaḥ/
    ø yen sirameta riṅ luhuṙriṅ wukiṙ nora kapaƞgiḥ jatiniṅ śabda, tapa boƞoḥ kaky arane hawis kaṅ wruḥ halaku jumnĕƞā/ saṅ wru riṅ gati saṅ tapa meƞadiya, tan kabĕteṅ wuwus mewĕ kaṅ jati wikana, nadyan hudakṣinahā denipunkari/ tan amāƞgiḥha lampaḥ
    ø lwiḥ hutamaniṅ tapa saṅ wruḥ pamutusi tapa di ta pṛnaḥhaihiya panḍitarane nora bawa saṅ ṛsi muliḥ tutuṙ/ walakā tan saṅsaya hame tann aƞel kasniṅ tapa, śira saṅƞ amet kasidan., haƞumanduṙma lawaṙ brata niṙ kabeḥ sena/ka muṙwwa kitri jati pralina tanpa mastu galaṙre
    ø kaliṅƞane wuwusku kaki hawis tuhwaniṅƞ amaƞun tapa, akwe wiku papa
    Folio 6v rante     kalawisaya ginuṅ kanuragan kaṅ denulati hawis amruḥha śonya, haƞi kawiṙyyan denguṅ haƞukwiḥ daṙmma kala/ban mayoga samady amriḥ wijili kitri daṙmma kaśukawakwan.
    ø tuhu panutuniṅ hyaṅ hamṛdi ki paƞuwusan., n ada/n awaraḥ sawƞi tan ana kule ki siƞamadḍa muwus rani aki winaraḥ jati haywage kumaliƞa, sawaṅn iṅ pamuwus./ mewĕḥ kaṅ jatw awaraha twasniṅ rasā masa wuruƞa kapaƞgiḥ, lamon. kṙtasamaya
    ø waniḥ saṅ wruḥ wiwaraniṅƞ aji ti/nata glariṅ mahapadma, pann iya hiku ḍapure pati patitisipun pik winaṙna rakutiṅ kawi pupuse kumalamaṙ wwi/te makin tan wruḥ hawis bapa kaṅ wikana, saṅƞ atapā riṅ sukma jñana wirati wruḥ panuƞgaliṅ śabda
    ø prasidakna lampaḥta/ kaki husinĕn. sira saṅ yogiśwara, saṅ mahapurusa wri reḥ, hana pamitraniṅsun halampaḥhi munindra lwiḥ maka/diniṅ prawata, kaṅ minaka guru, liganiṅƞ adi patapan., śukla pawitra wiku bramanacari jajaka hudaksina
    ø śakti
    Folio 7r wiśesa riṅ brata lwiḥ     kaṅ minakā purohitaniṅƞ atapa, sḍĕṅ tilasĕniṅƞ akwe haƞi ta hanakiṅsun., dipunbakti hana/mpa wasik dasasila dekna, hulat dentumukul., talatdanta metawĕḥ riṅƞ amet nug̈raha, kula hilaṅ bapa riṅƞ ameka/t kadadin haƞel. rala naspaha
    ø priḥ waṅsitira saṅ daṙmmajati petĕn sarasaniṅƞ adidrawa, kobalag̈ni huru/be śurupa tan katuduḥ kuruƞan mas tanpa cantri, paśuk. wta wtuniṅ tiga kabutan ṣuwuṅ kuwo muni ƞambara, takonakĕn siƞama/da hayo lali wkasi paḍaṅƞ awa

    ø ki daṙmmakaww aparemut gadgada wṛdaya niki, hĕntiṅ larane hatine taƞisira sajalestrī śig̈ra tu/luṅ sawane denkuśwakuśwa sawanne paran pwalaḥhira nini, tanpa sakan hĕmassisun hatiƞgal. brataniṅƞ ati

    ø taƞeḥ kawaṙnnaniṅ laku larane ki daṙmmakawi, śampun binniśeka make layonira saṅ taruni, sapalini palastra, pag̈aƞla
    Folio 84rƞan wusumaji     linasla.tararekakĕn ṣampun gumĕṛḥ śwaraniṅ taƞis.
    ø muṙtiniṅ rag̈a kawuwus ṣarira mbat aƞliḥ lakw alon aƞadehade ḷƞĕṅni tṛsna/ ladulu kalaƞĕniṅ janapada, kasmaran ni tejasari lampas lampaḥnya hadaruṅ mantuk waluya sulastri
    ø śaṅ supraba tujuṅbiru, sakweniṅ hyaṅhyaṅ tansari śa/kendra tusṭa manahe karunatisaya nusuṅ saṅ kuranta mawancana, kakaṅ saṅ tuñjuṅputiḥ bag̈ya kita yen rawuh paripuṙna mawakitri
    ø saṅ lambe/mĕnuṙr anuṅsuṅ saṅ gag̈aṙmmayaṅ tan kari, saṅ nilotama rowwaṅƞe lwan saṅ ḷṅḷṅmandanu, kaliḥ saṅ wara menaka, saṅ prabasiny atuṙr asiḥ kamayaƞan hatĕ/nku saṅ tuñjuṅputiḥ
    ø hana tapsari hahibu sumuṅsuṅƞa ri saṅ prapti hadan paywas lumakw age hasasampuṙ hidĕṙ lumbuṅ mĕgĕp asiñjaṅ wawara, ha/gehag̈e sayanipun., lumaku hamĕgaḥmiguḥ hilehilene tann ĕntiṅ
    ø wusnya sĕsṛbĕṅ kucubuṅ widane hapu lan kuniṙ hasusumpiṅ padma piƞe/ hawirag̈a luṅƞiṅ gaḍuṅ hasipat. bot lalakaran. ø motoros gatraniṅ pipi papantĕśe tann asurud lumaku haƞumikumik.
    ø ha/limbeyan ṛnjaḥṛnjaḥ hamolaḥhakĕnn awake hakol asekol. polaḥhe milupra hiƞ apet iñjuḥ lumaku haƞikaḥhikaḥ mesĕm ṣakweḥ
    Folio 84vniṅ tapsari     prapta heṅ saṅ sinuṅsuṅ ṛmwa mijaḥ hamkul ṣiḥ
    ø hamwĕḥha śuka katmu sakendran hanotani, sampun biniśeka rame kinulawisudeṅƞ a/yu rinuwat iṅƞ gag̈a tiṙta, ya śaka riṅ kunḍi manik., tumandeṅ śukma hayu, datan kawaṙnaha maniṅ
    ø rag̈asamaya wisanuwus. dennira ƞuśi kapatin./ hamriḥ sidahaniṅ gawe tumutuṙreṅ kakaṅƞipun. haƞiṅ masa katkana, gƞĕṅ saƞaraniṅ bummi mapan sampun tinuduḥ gumlariti riṅ tig̈a mukti
    ø /tlasniṅ byaktwa kalaƞon ka tikĕl tanaḥ hiƞ agurit ki sunata wri rame harañcana ƞapus laƞu kasmaran. brati wikal.pa, sawasiṅƞ alampaḥhi kataman tṛ/sna lulut ṣinamun iṅ dora wisṭi
    ø karananiṅƞ aƞapus kalaƞĕniṅ wṛdaya mriḥ saṅsipta kweḥ pamtune haƞiṅ tan ana niṅ laku winawa riṅ śoƞaṙ gawa,/ karane sa budi karasmin jumawa g̈agawe guyu waceni de saṅ pra kawi
    ø dĕg̈niṅ dwapara winaƞun hantakarana ginurit haṙtwiniṅ jaba daḷmme hiśi/niṅ gita tĕtĕlu, lanaṅ roro wadon tuṅgal kaṅƞ araniṅtejasari śurajaya kaṅ ketuṅ rag̈asamaya ginupi
    ø hantakaranarannipun kapi ṙwanira/ winĕṙtri, wirasanĕn wirasansae danadi laman ana wruḥ, sira riṅ kapw ana maca, kaṅƞ aripta denniṅ talib maṅmaṅ yoṅ lagi kabutuḥ hupaswaṙg̈a duruṅ kawi

    Folio 85r ø tlas diwasaniṅ laƞu     paguywaniṅƞ añampahi śabda tann ana tlage nadyan oliḥya sapikul. halusa roniṅ siwalan tan ana wipala ni/ki, wṛdaḥ bañcana manuḥhi saƞuniṅƞ awṛdi hati
    ø śuklapakṣa nika m kaṙtwika wuku manahil dite manis was tujone śri hasṭawaraniṅ/ wuku, catuṙwara nuju jaya, kahuwusanniṅƞ agurit kapayuheṅ saṅ putus. reḥniṅ raṙwa nom kumawi
    ø itiḥ śura/jaya dapuṙ hatĕmbaṅ mahisalaƞit hantakarana wkase hamṛdi hantuk paṅlaku ri tlasira cinitra, riṅ wijyatcala haspi, suśaḥ taṅ/ prawwata muṙ ḷƞkara makwa riṅ bummi
    ø mintane halawasuwuṅ sinukṛta polaḥ niki, denira saṅ tame kwatiṅ śara/t prawwaẗa rum riṅ sañjaya gwanya nurat haƞimuṙ budi karasmi maṙmmanya gugonn iṅ ḍukuḥ ḥaƞipuk. brataniṅƞ ati
    ø hatarukan ganya/ nusup. hasapi taln ana kampiṙ norana sudiƞ awake lagwa taẗarub sawuwuṙ sasakane kayu jarak hatĕpe/ roniṅ wariƞin tinap makwa denyalus. habcik lwiṙ sirap adi
    ø tikahe kadi tan luhuṅ hanom tan dṛman lampahi kneṅ guna biṣa
    Folio 85v ṛke     hujaṙrira saṅƞ anmu siptaniṅƞ antu nugraha, pjaḥ mati hurip maniṅ karane hajĕmuṙ winĕntaṙrakn iṅ kawi
    ø wikana ni/ra saṅ tambuḥ hahurip wikan. yen mati tĕtĕƞĕre heliṅ ṛke hanurat hantuk ṣasuru cinacaḥ haneṅ wawacan siptanira saṅƞ anu/lis duk lumaku kaya woṅ biƞuṅ mako sudamala niki
    ø niṙmmala gmut. yalampus niṙmala cipta mahniṅ kawastu tan iṅ wwaṅ/ƞ akweḥ siƞa maca suratisun haweya śuka warasa, jnĕkakneṅ wanidi śakti mantṛteṅ laku sumiwi heṅ wanagiri
    ø ra/ñcani kaww alaƞu rukal mareja g̈wan iki hakweḥ ƞatutuṙ haƞne haƞiṅ tan kaṙsaniṅ laku hamriḥ śunyaya śakṣana, pi/nĕḥ pawṛtti maniṅ haƞanti reḥhi smu walikaniṅ walaṅ mati
    ø titire sampun karuƞu wṛta pasaṙ hañampahi singuḥ manis gulane kalapa, winaweṅsarajuruḥ manis manisireṅ kilaṅ pyuḥ wutaḥ tumiḃeṅ sari ciptaniṅ haƞla ƞuru sinĕguḥ ḃa/ya hamanis.
    ø niskaraṇa sabda hiku kaṅwṛta sampun kaṅḃummi ḋenira saƞ anmu reḥ winor iƞ ulat lan guyu ḋene lamon ṣami wikan anista sampun karihi noraƞel ṣaƞ anmu gumlar i sila/yukti
